Abstract: Large language models deployed in open-world applications require safety guardrails that are both robust to complex risks and efficient enough for low-latency runtime moderation. Existing guardrails face a practical trade-off between lightweight classification-based models, which are efficient but often struggle with concealed intent, ambiguous semantics, and borderline safety decisions, and reasoning-based guards, which improve judgment quality but introduce additional token generation and inference latency. We present DT-Guard, a content safety guardrail model based on a Reasoning-Active Training, Reasoning-Free Inference paradigm. The key idea is to use reasoning supervision during training while emitting only structured safety labels at inference time. DT-Guard formulates safety judgment as a progressive decision process, Intent - Category - Safety, and constructs an intent-driven dataset with intent labels, risk categories, safety labels, and structured reasoning trajectories. To further improve hard-case robustness, we propose Rollout-Guided Progressive Hard-Case Optimization (RG-PHO), which uses multi-rollout consistency to identify stably mastered, persistently failed, and preference-unstable samples, and applies targeted supervised and preference optimization accordingly. At inference time, DT-Guard directly generates structured labels without explicit reasoning traces, preserving deployment efficiency. Experiments on prompt-side and response-side safety benchmarks show that DT-Guard achieves average F1 scores of 0.886 and 0.870, respectively. With only a 4B backbone, it reaches a dual-side average F1 of 0.878, outperforming strong 8B guardrail baselines. These results demonstrate that reasoning supervision can be effectively internalized into low-latency safety discrimination.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端自动驾驶模型日益复杂和黑箱化，存在学习到不良或错误行为的风险，亟需可解释性方法来揭示其决策逻辑。

Method: 提出逐步框架：1) 将无监督字典学习作为后验可解释性模块集成到驾驶模型中；2) 提取语义上有意义的概念并展示其对驾驶决策的因果影响；3) 在概念层面进行靶向干预，操纵和纠正驾驶决策。

Result: 概念层面的靶向干预能够操纵和纠正驾驶决策，带来整体驾驶性能的可测量提升。

Conclusion: 可解释性可以有效降低模型黑箱性、发现错误行为并进行靶向纠正，最终提升模型性能。

Abstract: The increasing adoption of end-to-end learning for autonomous driving introduces increased model complexity and opacity, raising the risk of learning undesired or erroneous behavior. In this work, we integrate unsupervised dictionary learning as a post hoc interpretability module within state-of-the-art driving models to decompose driving behavior into semantically meaningful concepts while demonstrating their causal influence on the model's driving decisions. We propose a stepwise framework for extracting and interpreting meaningful concepts from the end-to-end model and connecting them to the multifaceted model outputs, thereby revealing the underlying decision-making logic for the prediction of future trajectories. Furthermore, targeted interventions at the concept level allow us to manipulate and correct driving decisions, resulting in measurable improvements in overall driving performance. We thus demonstrate how interpretability can effectively be used to reduce model opacity, uncover erroneous behavior, and enable targeted mitigation, ultimately boosting model performance.

TopoBrick uses building knowledge graphs to construct a compact structural skeleton and employs an agentic topology sampler to select target-specific exogenous variables. The selected variables are organized by deployment-time availability, separating past-known sensor states from future-known calendar, schedule, and meteorological exogenous variables. Across three real-world buildings, TopoBrick outperforms strong zero-shot foundation-model baselines and remains competitive with fully trained building-specific models. Ablations show that topology-aware sampling is more reliable than random, ontology-only, or fixed-hop selection, especially for physically coupled HVAC and weather-driven sensing variables.

### [101] [ExplAIner: A Declarative Query Language for Explaining Classification Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06407)
*Marcelo Arenas,Pablo Barceló,Diego Bustamante,Jose Caraball,María Alejandra Schild,Bernardo Subercaseaux*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对可解释AI中众多解释概念缺乏统一查询语言的问题，提出了ExplAIner查询语言。该语言基于FOIL扩展而来，能够表达包括反事实、对比、特征和距离查询在内的广泛解释概念。作者证明了ExplAIner的评估问题在布尔模型类上属于布尔层次结构，而Opt-FOIL片段可在FP^NP中求解，这意味着只需固定次数的SAT求解器调用即可评估查询。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可解释AI领域涌现了大量不同类型的解释查询和评分方法，但从数据管理角度看，缺乏一种统一的声明式查询语言来规范地描述、组合和分析这些解释概念。现有工作FOIL虽然是一种可解释性查询语言，但存在两个根本局限：无法表达基于最优性的核心解释查询，且其评估问题在决策树上对多项式层次的每一层都是困难的。

Method: 论文首先重新审视了FOIL查询语言，指出其局限。随后提出ExplAIner，这是一种基于FOIL扩展的、具有分层结构的声明式查询语言，扩展了词汇表以支持更丰富的解释概念。进一步引入Opt-FOIL，这是ExplAIner的一个面向优化的片段，用于计算关于严格偏序的最小解释。理论分析上，论文证明了ExplAIner中每个查询的评估问题在特定布尔模型类上属于布尔层次结构，Opt-FOIL的评估问题在相同可解性假设下属于FP^NP。

Result: ExplAIner能够表达包括溯因解释、对比解释、基于特征的解释和基于距离的解释在内的广泛解释概念。评估问题方面，对于确定性且可分解的布尔电路等模型类，只要基本谓词可在多项式时间内评估，ExplAIner中的每个查询属于布尔层次结构，Opt-FOIL属于FP^NP。算法上，固定ExplAIner查询可通过固定次数的SAT求解器调用完成评估，Opt-FOIL指定的解释概念可通过多项式次数的SAT调用计算。

Conclusion: ExplAIner提供了统一的形式化框架来描述和分析多种解释概念，弥补了FOIL的不足。该工作将可解释AI与数据库查询语言、计算复杂度理论紧密联系起来，为形式化XAI中基于SAT求解器的解释计算提供了理论保证。未来可进一步扩展至更复杂的模型类和优化目标。

Abstract: The XAI community has studied a wide range of queries and scores for explaining predictions of ML models. From a data management perspective, this proliferation of explanation notions calls for declarative query languages in which such notions can be specified, combined, and analyzed uniformly. In this paper, we develop such a framework for Boolean models. We first revisit FOIL, an interpretability query language for black-box models, and show that it has two fundamental limitations: it cannot express central optimality-based explanation queries, and its evaluation problem over decision trees is hard for every level of the polynomial hierarchy. We then introduce ExplAIner, a query language based on FOIL with an extended vocabulary and a layered structure. We show that ExplAIner can express a broad family of explanation notions, including abductive, contrastive, feature-based, and distance-based queries. We also prove that the evaluation problem for each query in ExplAIner belongs to the Boolean hierarchy over every class of Boolean models for which some basic predicates can be evaluated in polynomial time. In particular, that property holds for deterministic and decomposable Boolean circuits. Finally, we introduce Opt-FOIL, an optimization-oriented fragment of ExplAIner for computing explanations that are minimal with respect to strict partial orders, and prove that its evaluation problem is in $\mathrm{FP}^{\mathrm{NP}}$ under the same tractability assumptions. These complexity results have a direct algorithmic consequence: a fixed ExplAIner query can be evaluated with a fixed number of calls to a SAT solver, while a notion of explanation specified in Opt-FOIL can be computed with a polynomial number of such calls. This is particularly relevant in formal XAI, where SAT solvers have been successfully used to compute explanations for several classes of ML models.

</details>


### [102] [Finding H. pylori in the Fine Print: Evidence-Linked Multi-Agent Case Finding from Gastric Biopsy Reports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06435)
*Yufan Wang,Anit Kumar Sahu,Yan Fei Ng,Daniel Kang,Shayan Vassef,Soorya Ram Shimgekar,Koustuv Saha,Piyum Zonooz,Navin Kumar,Chee Leong Cheng,Li Yan Khor*

TL;DR: 本文评估了Nimblemind多智能体系统(nMAS)在胃活检病理报告中提取H. pylori感染相关信息的表现。在216个特征-案例决策中，nMAS准确率98.61%，并展示了工作流集成和可追溯性优势，而非预测性能优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: H. pylori感染与慢性胃炎、消化性溃疡和胃癌相关，但其病理报告中相关信息分散在异构的编码和自由文本字段中，需要上下文解释断言和否定，关键词搜索受限，人工审核难以规模化。

Method: 回顾性试点评估，使用54份去标识化胃活检病理报告，通过nMAS（字段名驱动、证据链接的提取工作流）评估四个二值字段：胃/胃活检、活检状态、H. pylori阳性、H. pylori相关胃炎。与UMA-style MiniMax M2.5比较器对比。

Result: 216个特征-案例决策中正确分类213个，准确率98.61%。与比较器性能相似，但nMAS保持统一报告级输出并附带支持源句子。模拟场景下，审核1000份报告可从83.3工时降至1.4工时，节省约6,100美元。

Conclusion: nMAS的贡献在于工作流集成和可追溯性，而非预测性能优势。需更大规模多机构研究评估证据跨度正确性、临床医生验证时间和泛化性。

Abstract: Data from Singapore indicated that about 31% of the population had evidence of Helicobacter pylori infection. Persistent H. pylori infection is associated with chronic active gastritis and peptic ulcer disease, and its eradication is key to gastric cancer prevention. However, evidence supporting \textit{H. pylori} positivity and H. pylori-associated gastritis may be distributed across heterogeneous coded and free-text report fields and may require contextual interpretation of assertion and negation, limiting keyword search, and making manual review difficult to scale. We conducted a retrospective pilot evaluation of the Nimblemind Multi-Agent System (nMAS), a field-name-driven, evidence-linked extraction workflow, using 54 de-identified gastric biopsy pathology reports from a large healthcare system in Singapore. Four clinician-scoped binary fields were evaluated: gastric/stomach biopsy, biopsy status, H. pylori positivity, and H. pylori-associated gastritis. Across 216 feature-case decisions, nMAS correctly classified 213, corresponding to 98.61% overall accuracy. A separately implemented UMA-style MiniMax M2.5 comparator produced similar aggregate and per-field classification metrics. Although predictive performance was similar, nMAS maintained unified report-level outputs with supporting source sentences; the demonstrated contribution is therefore workflow integration and traceability rather than predictive superiority. Under an illustrative, unmeasured scenario, reviewing 1,000 reports at five minutes per manual review versus five seconds per evidence-linked verification would reduce review time from 83.3 to 1.4 staff-hours, corresponding to 81.9 staff-hours and about USD~6,100 in potential staff-time value. Larger multi-institutional studies should evaluate evidence-span correctness, clinician verification time, and generalizability.

### [103] [Danus: Orchestrating Mathematical Reasoning Agents with Fact-Graph Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06447)
*Jihao Liu,Guoxiong Gao,Zeming Sun,Bin Wu,Shurui Liu,Jiedong Jiang,Haocheng Ju,Leheng Chen,Ronnie Cheng,Xiping Zhang,Bin Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Danus 是一个基于事实图（fact graph）作为全局内存管理机制的数学推理编排系统，通过主Agent规划、多个Worker并行证明搜索和静态验证器检查，能够构建长篇详细数学证明，在代数几何、奇点理论和组合学等六个研究级案例中验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的数学推理Agent虽然已能处理研究级问题甚至解决开放问题，但在规模化编排多个Agent时面临并行证明搜索难以协调、中间主张难以组织和保持可靠性的挑战。

Method: Danus包含一个负责规划和协调的主Agent、多个并行执行证明搜索的Worker Agent，以及一个在数学主张被纳入事实图前进行校验的无状态验证器。每个验证后的事实连同其证明和逻辑依赖关系一起存储，主Agent定期总结证明状态、重定向Worker，并支持与人类数学家的交互。

Result: 通过代数几何、奇点理论和组合学等六个研究级案例研究，展示了事实图内存机制使Danus能够构建长篇详细的数学证明。代码已在GitHub开源。

Conclusion: 基于事实图的编排为扩展面向长周期研究问题的数学推理Agent提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Recent LLM-based mathematical reasoning agents have begun to tackle research-level problems and, in several cases, have contributed to the resolution of open problems. However, scaling and orchestrating such agents effectively remains challenging, due to the difficulty of coordinating parallel proof search while keeping intermediate claims organized and reliable. In this paper, we propose Danus, an orchestration system for research-level mathematical reasoning centered on a shared fact graph as a global memory-management mechanism. Danus consists of a main agent that performs planning and coordination, multiple worker agents that carry out proof search in parallel, and a stateless verifier that checks proposed mathematical claims before they are admitted into the fact graph. Each verified fact is stored together with its proof and logical dependencies, allowing the system to build long arguments incrementally while keeping the shared proof state organized. The main agent periodically summarizes the evolving proof state, redirects workers across promising directions, and supports interaction with human mathematicians through progress reports. We evaluate Danus through six research-level case studies in algebraic geometry, singularity theory, and combinatorics, illustrating how the fact-graph memory mechanism enables Danus to construct long, detailed mathematical proofs. Our results suggest that fact-graph-based orchestration provides an effective route toward scaling mathematical reasoning agents for long-horizon research problems. Danus is open source at https://github.com/frenzymath/Danus.

### [104] [A Physics-Informed Neural Network Framework for Elastodynamic Wave Propagation in Bimaterial Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06479)
*Sonal Ankush Chibire,Jenn-Terng Gau,Bo Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于物理信息神经网络（PINNs）的框架，用于模拟双材料系统中的瞬态弹性波传播。该框架将控制方程、初始/边界/界面条件直接嵌入损失函数，利用ANSYS有限元仿真数据验证，成功预测了波在钢-铝界面的透射与反射行为，并可作为连续代理模型推广至不同材料组合和时间点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值方法（如有限元）求解弹性波传播问题计算成本高，且难以灵活推广到新材料或时间点。研究旨在利用PINN将物理定律直接嵌入网络训练，构建一个准确、高效且可连续采样的代理模型，替代部分昂贵的数值仿真。

Method: 构建PINN框架，将轴对称线弹性控制方程、初始条件、边界条件及界面连续性条件整合到网络损失函数中。采用高速率有限元分析（ANSYS Explicit Dynamics）生成高保真数据用于训练约束和验证。网络训练后在时间域和材料参数空间上形成连续可微的代理模型。

Result: 模型准确预测了双材料界面处的波透射与反射，轴向/径向位移历史、面平均响应及主应力/应变演化均与有限元解高度吻合。训练后的网络可预测未见时间点及修改材料属性后的波响应。网格敏感性验证了数值鲁棒性，多材料组合证明了方法通用性。

Conclusion: 将物理信息神经网络与显式有限元分析结合，为异质固体中的弹性波传播提供了准确且计算高效的框架。该方法可作为高应变率固体力学与冲击工程中有效的代理建模工具，显著减少对大规模数值仿真的依赖。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) provide a promising framework for solving partial differential equations while embedding the underlying physical laws directly into the learning process. This study presents a PINN-based framework for modeling transient elastodynamic wave propagation in bimaterial systems governed by the axisymmetric equations of linear elasticity. A steel-aluminum specimen representative of a Split Hopkinson Pressure Bar configuration is considered, and the governing elastodynamic equations, together with the corresponding initial, boundary, and interface conditions, are incorporated directly into the network through a physics-informed loss function. High-fidelity finite-element simulations performed using ANSYS Workbench Explicit Dynamics are used for validation and as supplementary data constraints during training. The proposed framework accurately predicts wave transmission and reflection across the bimaterial interface and reproduces axial and radial displacement histories, face-averaged responses, and the dominant stress and strain evolution with close agreement to the finite-element solutions. The trained network further demonstrates the ability to predict wave responses at previously unseen time instants and for modified material properties without requiring additional finite-element simulations, providing a continuous surrogate model for elastodynamic analysis. Mesh-sensitivity studies confirm numerical robustness, while additional material combinations demonstrate the generality of the proposed methodology. The results show that integrating physics-informed neural networks with explicit finite-element analysis provides an accurate and computationally efficient framework for elastodynamic wave propagation in heterogeneous solids, offering an effective surrogate modeling approach for high-rate solid mechanics and impact engineering applications.

### [106] [Doomed from the Start: Early Abort of LLM Agent Episodes via a Recall-Controlled Probe Cascade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06503)
*Kai Ruan,Zihe Huang,Ziqi Zhou,Qianshan Wei,Xuan Wang,Hao Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于LLM智能体内部隐藏表征的早期失败预测方法，通过每轮校准门控级联机制，在保证高召回率的前提下显著节省推理计算资源（最高节省47.1%），并证明了该方法优于仅基于行为观察的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在多步任务中经常执行注定失败的轨迹，但仍消耗大量推理计算资源，直到失败变得明显。本文旨在通过早期预测失败来节省这些浪费的计算资源。

Method: 1）在每轮交互中，从智能体内部隐藏激活状态训练轻量级探针来预测最终失败；2）构建每轮校准门控级联（abort cascade），通过联合搜索每轮召回率预算，保证最终成功的情节以用户指定的全局概率通过所有门控；3）引入分布无关的校准方法确保门控的有效性。

Result: 在TextCraft上，针对Qwen-2.5-7B和Llama-3.2-3B两种模型，级联方法在90%-97%召回率目标下均满足要求；在90%召回率目标下，分别节省47.1%±10.3%和37.2%±8.8%的推理计算量，是最优单门控策略的1.6-1.7倍。仅基于行为观察的方案节省量约为一半，添加行为特征到探针中无额外收益。

Conclusion: 智能体内部隐藏表征比行为观察能更早、更准确地预测失败，转化为实际计算节省效果显著；本文还刻画了认证高召回率目标的样本复杂度，为实践者提供数据可行性指导。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents solving multi-step tasks frequently commit to trajectories that are doomed to fail, yet continue to consume substantial inference compute before the failure becomes observable. We show that failure is predictable early from the agent's internal representations: lightweight per-round probes on hidden activations anticipate eventual episode failure as early as the first interaction round, where scorers reading only the agent's observable behavior are barely better than chance. We turn this signal into a practical abort cascade: one distribution-free calibrated gate per round, with per-round recall budgets jointly searched so that eventually-successful episodes survive all gates at a user-specified global rate; this episode-level guarantee is the one that matters in deployment, since false-abort risk accumulates across gates. Across two agent models on TextCraft, the cascade meets every recall target from 90% to 97% and, at the 90% target, saves 47.1% +/- 10.3% (Qwen-2.5-7B) and 37.2% +/- 8.8% (Llama-3.2-3B) of inference compute, 1.6--1.7x the best single-gate policy. An otherwise-identical cascade reading only behavior saves roughly half as much, and adding behavioral features to the probe yields no further gain: the hidden states capture what behavior reveals. Finally, we characterize the sample complexity of certifying high recall targets, telling practitioners which recall promises their data can, and provably cannot, back. The code will be released soon.

</details>


### [107] [RMISC: A Large-scale Real-world Multivariate Corpus for Time Series Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06504)
*Qian Sun,Yong-Ming Tian,Jia-Wei Huang,Cheng Feng,Shao-Qun Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文构建了大规模真实多变量时间序列语料库RMISC，并通过实验证明：使用真实多变量数据预训练的时间序列基础模型，其零样本泛化能力显著优于使用合成多变量数据训练的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列基础模型主要依赖合成多变量数据进行预训练，但合成数据可能无法捕捉真实时间序列中复杂的时序动态和跨变量关系。作者旨在探究使用真实世界语料训练的模型是否优于合成数据训练的模型，并为此构建大规模真实多变量时间序列语料库。

Method: 1) 构建RMISC语料库：包含约200个数据集、1420亿个时间点的大规模高质量真实多变量时间序列档案；2) 在单变量、合成多变量和真实多变量三种数据上预训练四种先进TSFM；3) 在标准分布内和分布外基准上评估模型的零样本泛化能力。

Result: 使用真实多变量数据预训练能显著提升单变量和多变量TSFM的泛化性能，表明真实数据比合成数据对模型学习更有效。

Conclusion: 真实世界多变量数据对于开发更强的时间序列基础模型具有重要贡献价值，为未来TSFM的数据策略提供了指导方向。

Abstract: Recent years have witnessed the emergence of multivariate modeling using time series foundation models (TSFMs), which achieve advanced zero-shot generalization. Modern multivariate TSFMs are predominantly pretrained on multivariate synthetic data, which is easier to scale but may fail to capture the complex temporal dynamics and cross-variable relationships present in real-world time series. This raises a key question: Whether and to what extent the leading TSFMs trained with the real-world corpus perform better than those trained with synthetic data? To answer this, we establish the RMISC corpus, a considerably large-scale, high-quality, openly accessible, real-world, and multivariate time series archive that contains around 200 datasets and 142 billion time points across diverse domains. Furthermore, we pretrain four advanced TSFMs on univariate, synthetic multivariate, and real-world multivariate data and evaluate their zero-shot generalization capabilities on standard in-distribution and out-of-distribution benchmarks. Experimental results show that incorporating real-world multivariate data predominantly improves the generalization performance for both univariate and multivariate TSFMs. These results provide a deeper understanding of how real-world multivariate data contributes to the development of stronger TSFMs.

### [108] [FootsiesGym: A Fighting Game Benchmark for Two-Player Zero-Sum Imperfect-Information Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06514)
*Chase McDonald,Nathan Tsang,Wesley N. Kerr*

TL;DR: FootsiesGym是一个基于2D格斗游戏Footsies的开源环境，用于研究非平凡双人零和不完美信息博弈中的学习问题。它隔离了格斗游戏中循环、非传递性的战略交互，提供了向量化模拟器支持高效训练，并基准测试了多种强化学习算法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习环境要么过于简单缺乏战略交互，要么过于复杂难以分析和复现。格斗游戏的"中立博弈"（neutral play）具有循环克制、非传递性的战略结构，是研究此类博弈的理想载体，但缺少一个简洁、高效、可复现的环境。

Method: 基于HiFight的极简2D格斗游戏Footsies构建环境，提取其中立博弈的核心机制（攻防循环与策略克制关系）。提供向量化模拟器（vectorized simulator）以支持标准硬件上的高吞吐量训练，并集成了多种强化学习算法的基准测试实现。

Result: 成功构建了一个兼具非平凡战略深度与计算效率的环境，能够在标准硬件上进行高效训练和可复现的实验。通过多种RL算法的基准测试，验证了环境的可用性，揭示了该环境下不同算法的表现差异。

Conclusion: FootsiesGym为研究双人零和不完美信息博弈中的循环非传递性策略交互提供了一个理想的测试平台，填补了现有环境在"简单但非平凡"之间的空白，并开启了多个有前景的研究方向。

Abstract: We present FootsiesGym, an open-source environment for learning in a non-trivial two-player, zero-sum, imperfect-information game. Built on HiFight's minimalist 2D fighting game Footsies, it isolates the cyclic, non-transitive strategic interactions of fighting game neutral play while remaining simple enough for efficient analysis. We provide a vectorized simulator that enables high-throughput training on standard hardware, making the environment accessible and reproducible. We describe the design of the environment, benchmark several reinforcement learning algorithms, and discuss open research directions it enables. The code is available at https://github.com/como-research/FootsiesGym.

### [109] [FreqDepthKV: Frequency-Guided Depth Sharing for Robust KV Cache Compression in Long-Context LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06519)
*Anna Córdoba,Adam Puente Tercero,Nerea Angulo Hijo,Mar Linares Tercero,Julia Barrientos,Ainhoa Miranda,Jesús Olivera*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FreqDepthKV 是一种推理时 KV 缓存压缩方法，通过将相邻层状态分解为共享低频深度分量和稀疏高频残差，并动态分配注意力头到不同缓存模式，在 32k token 窗口下达到 3.9x 有效压缩率，同时保持推理质量并提升吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文 LLM 推理中 KV 缓存的内存和带宽成本日益成为瓶颈，但过度压缩会丢失层特定的证据，影响检索和多步推理能力。现有方法往往在压缩率与任务性能之间难以兼顾。

Method: 将相邻层的 KV 状态分解为共享的低频深度分量（低频共享信息）和稀疏的高频残差（层特有信息）；通过轻量级在线探针，根据注意力头对重构敏感 Logits 的贡献，动态分配头到共享深度、残差深度或精确缓存三种模式。

Result: 在长上下文问答、Needle 检索、摘要和代码生成任务上，32k 窗口下 Exact Match 58.3、F1 63.0、ROUGE-L 32.5、pass@1 48.1；吞吐量 70.4 tokens/s、TTFT 2.06 秒、峰值 KV 内存 6.2 GB，有效压缩率 3.9x，优于先前压缩缓存方法。

Conclusion: FreqDepthKV 通过深度-残差分解与自适应缓存模式分配，在不重训练的前提下实现了高压缩率下的任务精度保持，为长上下文 LLM 的高效推理提供了一种有效方案。

Abstract: Long-context LLM inference is increasingly limited by the memory and bandwidth cost of KV caches, yet aggressive compression can remove the layer-specific evidence needed for retrieval and multi-step reasoning. We introduce FreqDepthKV, an inference-time cache compression method that factorizes adjacent-layer KV states into shared low-frequency depth components and sparse high-frequency residuals. A lightweight online probe assigns attention heads to shared-depth, residual-depth, or exact cache modes according to their contribution to reconstruction-sensitive attention logits, allowing the compression policy to adapt to prompt structure without retraining. Across long-context question answering, needle retrieval, summarization, and code generation benchmarks, FreqDepthKV preserves task accuracy under substantially smaller cache budgets. With a 32k-token prefill window, FreqDepthKV reaches 58.3 Exact Match, 63.0 F1, 32.5 ROUGE-L, and 48.1 pass@1, closely matching full KV while outperforming prior compressed-cache methods. It also improves decoding throughput to 70.4 tokens/s, reduces TTFT to 2.06 seconds, and lowers peak KV memory to 6.2 GB, achieving a 3.9x effective compression ratio.

</details>


### [110] [Bridging Physical Reasoning and Task Generalization via Visual Action Outcome Reasoning Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06522)
*Han-Jun Ko,Jr-Jen Chen,Haobo Yuan,Hsin-Ying Lee,Tiancheng Shen,Ming-Hsuan Yang,Yu-Chiang Frank Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: VAORA通过视觉对齐奖励和视觉-动作对齐奖励，抑制VLM在物理推理中的幻觉链式思维，并弥合推理与行动之间的差距，在PHYRE和Virtual Tool任务上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM在交互式物理推理中泛化能力差，存在两大问题：1）推理链与物理现实矛盾的幻觉；2）模型推理与实际行动不对齐。

Method: 提出VAORA奖励设计，包含两种互补奖励：视觉对齐奖励（将推理锚定于视觉上下文，独立于动作）和视觉-动作对齐奖励（将推理基于动作导致的视觉结果）。通过预训练专家模型估计成功概率，实现平滑密集奖励以提升训练稳定性。

Result: 在PHYRE和Virtual Tool基准上，VAORA在新任务和未见环境设置中均取得了优异表现。

Conclusion: 通过VAORA可以诱导出具有基础感知能力和良好泛化性的物理智能。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) struggle to generalize in interactive physical reasoning, particularly under unseen tasks and environments. Two key failure modes are prominent: hallucinated chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning that contradicts physical reality, and misalignment between the model's reasoning and actions. We present VAORA (Visual Action Outcome Reasoning Alignment), a novel reward design that directly addresses both issues. VAORA introduces two complementary rewards: Visual Alignment Reward, which anchors VLM reasoning to the visual context independent of the agent action itself, and Visual-Action Alignment Reward, which grounds reasoning in the visual outcome induced by the model's action. Together, these rewards suppress hallucinated CoT and reduce the gap between reasoning and behavior. To improve training stability, we further employ smooth, dense rewards by estimating success probabilities using a pre-trained in-domain expert agent. Experiments on PHYRE and Virtual Tool support our performances across novel-task and unseen-environment settings, confirming that grounded and generalizable physical intelligence can be induced through VAORA.

</details>


### [111] [DepthWeave-KV: Token-Adaptive Cross-Layer Residual Factorization for Long-Context KV Cache Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06523)
*Anna Cordoba,Adam Puente Tercero,Nerea Angulo Hijo,Mar Linares Tercero,Julia Barrientos,Ainhoa Miranda,Jesus Olivera*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DepthWeave-KV是一种令牌自适应缓存压缩方法，通过跨层低秩共享基和令牌特定残差来压缩KV缓存，在保持高任务质量的同时实现8.3倍内存压缩和72.8 tok/s的推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文语言模型推理受限于KV缓存的内存带宽和容量，现有压缩方法通常对层或令牌应用统一预算，导致在需要不同保存策略的词汇线索和语义状态下检索性能下降。

Method: 1) 跨深度残差分解：跨相邻Transformer层共享低秩通道基；2) 令牌条件深度路由器：为指令承载型和检索关键型令牌分配更高重建秩；3) 无需校准的在线误差追踪：利用注意力输出探针在生成过程中自适应调整压缩。

Result: 在LongBench、Needle-in-a-Haystack、L-Eval等基准测试中接近全缓存任务质量，平均得分和检索准确率优于此前压缩缓存方法，实现8.3倍KV内存缩减，64K上下文下达到72.8 tokens/s。

Conclusion: DepthWeave-KV通过令牌自适应的跨层分解与在线误差追踪，在不重训练模型的前提下有效平衡了缓存压缩率与推理质量，为长上下文LLM的高效部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Long-context language model inference is increasingly limited by the memory bandwidth and capacity required to store key-value caches, yet existing compression methods often apply uniform budgets across layers or tokens and degrade retrieval when lexical cues and semantic states require different preservation. We introduce DepthWeave-KV, a token-adaptive cache compression method that factorizes key and value states across neighboring transformer layers using shared low-rank channel bases while retaining lightweight token-specific residuals where attention behavior is sensitive. DepthWeave-KV combines cross-depth residual factorization with a token-conditional depth router that allocates higher reconstruction rank to instruction-bearing and retrieval-critical tokens, and uses calibration-free online error tracking from attention-output probes to adapt compression during generation without retraining the base model. A fused CUDA implementation jointly performs basis lookup, residual dequantization, and attention projection to reduce decode-time memory traffic. Across LongBench, Needle-in-a-Haystack, L-Eval, and long-form QA and summarization benchmarks, DepthWeave-KV achieves near-full-cache task quality with substantially lower memory use, improving average score and retrieval accuracy over prior compressed caches while reaching 8.3x KV memory reduction and 72.8 tokens per second at 64K context.

</details>


### [112] [The Large Cancer Assistant (LCA): A Model-Agnostic Orchestration Framework for Scalable Clinical Decision Support in Oncology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06531)
*Ghassen Marrakchi,Basarab Matei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了大型癌症助手（LCA），一个模型无关的事后编排框架，用于可扩展的临床决策支持。LCA通过7元组架构和算法不可渗透性原则，解耦多模态数据摄入与AI推理，并引入标准中间载荷（SIP）实现架构边界。概念验证在四个技术场景中验证了其编排逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前肿瘤学中的多模态深度学习模型采用单体式设计，数据摄入、临床路由和AI推理之间刚性耦合，缺乏灵活性。为突破这一限制，需要一种模型无关的、可扩展的编排框架。

Method: LCA采用7元组架构，基于算法不可渗透性原则（编排逻辑与底层黑箱AI模型严格独立）。引入基于几何深度学习的入口理论（Entry Theory）标准化多模态数据，通过癌症切换模块动态编排数据，输出标准中间载荷（SIP）隔离核心AI执行与易变的医院IT基础设施。

Result: 概念验证在四个技术场景中：名义流程中编排开销可忽略；AI模型切换时路由投影不变（验证算法不可渗透性）；数据异常下补充数据请求召回率达100%（验证严格故障安全性）；多协议执行能力也得到验证。

Conclusion: LCA通过结构性解耦多模态数据摄入与特征推理，提供了高度可适应的模块化编排基础。SIP建立了清晰的架构边界，为后续与其他系统（如EMR）的互操作性奠定了基础。

Abstract: - Objective: Multimodal deep learning models in oncology are currently limited by monolithic designs that rigidly couple data ingestion, clinical routing, and artificial intelligence (AI) inference. To address this inflexibility, we propose the Large Cancer Assistant (LCA), a model-agnostic, post-hoc orchestration framework designed for scalable clinical decision support. - Methods: The LCA is mathematically formalized as a 7-tuple architecture grounded in the principle of Algorithmic Impermeability, ensuring the orchestration logic remains strictly independent of underlying black-box AI models. We introduce the Entry Theory, leveraging Geometric Deep Learning (GDL) to standardize multimodal patient data along distinct structural and medical axes. The system dynamically orchestrates data via a Cancer Switching Module and intentionally isolates the core AI execution from volatile hospital IT infrastructures by outputting a Standardized Intermediate Payload (SIP). - Results: A Proof of Concept (PoC) validated the orchestration logic across four technical scenarios. The framework executed a nominal flow with negligible orchestration overhead. It empirically demonstrated algorithmic impermeability by maintaining an invariant routing projection during AI model swaps, and it validated strict failure-safety by achieving a 100\% recall rate in generating targeted Supplementary Data Requests (SDR) under injected data anomalies. Multi-protocol execution capability was also successfully verified. - Conclusion: By structurally decoupling multimodal ingestion from feature inference, the LCA provides a highly adaptable and modular orchestration foundation. The SIP establishes a clear architectural boundary, natively setting the stage for downstream Electronic Medical Record (EMR) interoperability as an independent future paradigm.

</details>

*Aparna Madva,Sharath Srivatsa,Srinath Srinivasa,Tulika Saha*

In this paper, we try to characterize this problem by addressing the extensive characteristic nature of Indian linguistics and the way they closely connect to cultural practices and worldview. We then perform a longitudinal survey of how Natural Language Processing (NLP) techniques have evolved in this space, tracing the historical development of Indic NLP, covering key milestones, methodological shifts, and resource creation efforts. In addition, the paper also examines the structural and sociolinguistic characteristics of Indian languages, such as rich morphology, complex scripts and grammar rules, diglossia, and large dialectal variation, and explains how these create unique challenges for building AI foundation models. We then discuss the growing role of Indic foundation models and analyze how these models address these long-standing resource and representation gaps. Finally, we propose a research direction called 'Culture Sensing', which re-imagines AI based on hermeneutic reasoning. Culture Sensing aims to address open problems such as ensuring equitable performance across low-resource languages and producing outputs that are culturally meaningful. By bringing together past work, current techniques, and emerging trends, this paper outlines research directions that can guide the next phase of Indic NLP and contribute to the development of more robust and inclusive Indic foundation models.

### [114] [Higher-Order Certified Robustness for Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05536)
*Jie Zhang,Natalie Frank*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出了面向回归任务的认证鲁棒框架，利用梯度信息构建预测中心化证书，在MNIST旋转任务上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机平滑在分类任务的鲁棒性认证上表现优异，但在回归任务中应用不足；现有回归证书依赖概率接受区域，未能有效利用函数的局部几何信息。

Method: 提出预测中心化证书框架，通过显式引入均值、方差和梯度信息来构造证书，特别是利用梯度信息生成更紧的鲁棒性保证。

Result: 在MNIST旋转任务上，利用梯度信息的证书相比基线方法alpha-smoothing获得了显著更紧的鲁棒性证书。

Conclusion: 提出的梯度感知证书框架有效解决了回归任务中鲁棒性认证的瓶颈，为回归场景下的认证鲁棒性提供了新思路。

Abstract: Randomized smoothing has emerged as a scalable technique for certifying the adversarial robustness of classifiers. However, its application to regression remains under-explored and faces unique challenges. Existing regression certificates rely on probabilistic acceptance regions and fail to exploit the local geometry of the function. In this work, we present a novel framework for certified robust regression that addresses these limitations. We derive a prediction-centered certificate that guarantees the stability of the smoothed model's prediction and ensures practical computability at test time. We investigate several alternatives for constructing these certificates by explicitly incorporating means, variances, and gradients. In particular, we demonstrate on the MNIST rotation task that utilizing gradient information yields significantly tighter robustness certificates compared to the current state-of-the-art, alpha-smoothing.

### [115] [Deep Neural Variation Spaces: A Unifying Perspective on Depth and Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05546)
*Julia Nakhleh,Robert D. Nowak*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了深度全连接神经网络的统一函数空间理论，通过递归的ℓ¹-有界线性组合定义函数空间，适用于多种激活函数（包括非齐次激活）。在单变量ReLU情况下证明了“深度饱和”现象：深度仅带来常数尺度的缩放，不增加功能多样性；深度控制的ReLU函数不能在高维任意方向上产生高频。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度网络理论大多局限于ReLU等齐次激活函数，缺乏一个统一的函数空间框架来刻画不同激活函数下深度网络的函数复杂度。作者希望建立一个通用的理论，连接基于范数的复杂度界、深度的变分刻画等不同研究方向。

Method: 定义递归函数空间：第一层为仿射函数字典，后续层为前一层激活函数的ℓ¹-有界线性组合。该构造统一了多种激活函数，并可用于分析深度范数约束网络所能表示的函数类型。

Result: 证明了新的表示定理和函数空间复杂度界；在单变量ReLU情况下证明深度饱和：深度仅带来常数缩放；证明了深度范数控制的ReLU函数在任何维度上不能沿任意方向产生高频。

Abstract: We develop a unified function space theory of deep fully connected neural networks. Functions in our spaces are defined recursively as $\ell^1$-bounded linear combinations of activated functions from preceding layers, with a dictionary of affine functions at the first layer. Unlike existing theories that are largely specialized to homogeneous activations such as the ReLU, our framework provides a meaningful notion of functional complexity for deep networks with a broad range of homogeneous and non-homogeneous activation functions commonly used in practice. This simple construction unites several seemingly disparate ideas from the literature, including norm-based complexity bounds and variational characterizations of depth, and facilitates novel analyses of what kinds of functions deep norm-constrained networks can represent. To this end, we prove a novel representer theorem for our spaces and establish novel function-space complexity bounds showing that the associated function classes remain qualitatively small at arbitrary depth. In the univariate ReLU case, we prove a "depth saturation" result: depth in this setting yields only a small constant rescaling of the function class, with no added functional diversity. As a consequence, we show that deep norm-controlled ReLU functions in any dimension cannot exhibit high frequencies along any direction. This finding reveals that some commonly cited expressivity benefits of depth disappear once network complexity is controlled by an appropriate function space norm, rather than parameter count or other representational costs that permit compounded rescaling across layers. Overall, our results illustrate how a function space perspective yields new structural insights into the relationship between depth and complexity.

### [116] [To Retain or to Adapt? Generalizing Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05609)
*Giulia Lanzillotta,Mandana Samiei,Doina Precup,Razvan Pascanu,Claire Vernade*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文挑战了持续学习中“以保留知识为核心”的传统假设，提出应关注平均终身误差（ALE），将持续学习形式化为在线优化问题。通过引入迁移效率（Transfer Efficiency）量化不稳定性和瞬态误差之间的张力，推导出关键任务持续时间（Critical Task Duration）阈值。实验验证了理论预测，并提出了预测性持续学习（Predictive CL）这一新算法家族。

Method: 1) 将持续学习形式化为以平均终身误差（ALE）为目标的在线优化问题；2) 提出迁移效率（Transfer Efficiency）量化不稳定性（继承自冲突经验的偏差）与瞬态误差（从零学习新任务的优化成本）之间的张力；3) 推导出关键任务持续时间（Critical Task Duration）的闭式阈值；4) 提出预测性持续学习（Predictive CL）算法家族，以Window算法为例在JTL和ITL之间插值。

Abstract: The Continual Learning (CL) literature has long been driven by the goal of mitigating catastrophic forgetting. This objective rests on a pervasive, often unstated assumption: that a lifelong learner should approximate the Joint-Task Learning (JTL) solution and retain all previously acquired knowledge. We challenge this retention-centered premise, arguing that in non-stationary environments prioritizing retention can impede real-time adaptation. Shifting the focus to the Average Lifelong Error (ALE), we formalize CL as an online optimization problem governed by the interaction between environmental and learning dynamics. We introduce Transfer Efficiency as a quantitative measure of the tension between Instability, the bias inherited from conflicting past experience, and Transient Error, the optimization cost of learning new tasks from scratch. Under mild convergence conditions, holding across linear and neural network models, this decomposition yields a Critical Task Duration: a closed-form threshold beyond which historical knowledge transitions from a warm-start advantage to an optimization liability whenever retention induces a positive stationary bias. We validate these theoretical predictions on continual image classification and reinforcement learning benchmarks. Finally, by connecting continual learning to the online learning framework of predictable sequences, we show that JTL is only one instance of a broader family of objectives, and we propose a new general class of continual learning algorithms, which we call Predictive Continual Learning. Predictive CL algorithms optimize expected future performance under an explicit, dynamically updated model of future tasks. As a proof of concept, we analyze a Window algorithm that interpolates between JTL and Independent-Task Learning (ITL), outperforming both under controlled distributional drift.

### [118] [Width-Robust Learnability in Mean-Field Bayesian Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05735)
*Dmitry Vaintrob,Kaarel Hänni*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究了贝叶斯神经网络在平均场（临界特征学习）缩放下的无限宽度极限，证明了有限宽度与无限宽度网络在归纳偏置上的等价性：一个目标函数族在无限宽度下可用多项式样本学习，当且仅当其在多项式宽度下可学习，当且仅当其约化熵是多项式有界的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无限宽度极限是分析神经网络的常用方法，但尚不清楚极限学习器是否与有限大宽度网络具有相同的复杂度理论归纳偏置。本文旨在解决这一关键问题。

Method: 引入约化熵（reduced entropy）作为核心量，衡量用先验表示目标函数到给定精度的代价。通过子采样（subsampling）方法证明：从无限宽度平均场解中，可同时选择多项式个代表性神经元，保留学习函数，分为"主动"（保留数据依赖的低维统计）和"惰性"（从先验重采样熵主导方向）两部分。

Result: 证明了宽度鲁棒可学习性定理：在固定深度下，布尔立方体目标函数族在无限宽度下可用多项式样本学习 ⇔ 在多项式宽度下可学习 ⇔ 其约化熵是多项式有界的。即，在多项式精度松弛下，贝叶斯平均场学习器恰好泛化到那些可由多项式大小网络表示的目标。

Conclusion: 无限宽度平均场极限为学习提供了简洁的解析描述，且不会引入虚假的宽度依赖泛化能力，验证了无限宽度极限与有限大宽度网络在归纳偏置上的一致性。

Abstract: Infinite-width limits are a standard way to reason about neural networks, but it is not automatic that the limiting learner has the same complexity-theoretic inductive bias as large finite networks. We study this question for Bayesian neural networks at the mean-field, or critical feature-learning, scaling. The central quantity is the \emph{reduced entropy} \[
  s_\infty(y,\varepsilon)=\limsup_N -\frac{1}{N}\log π_N^0(L\le \varepsilon), \] the intensive prior cost of representing a target function $y$ to population mean-squared error $\varepsilon$.
  Our main result is a width-robust learnability theorem. At fixed depth, a family of Boolean-cube targets is learnable from polynomially many samples at infinite width if and only if it is learnable at polynomial width, if and only if its reduced entropy is polynomially bounded. Equivalently, up to polynomial slack in accuracy, the Bayesian mean-field learner generalizes exactly on the targets that can be represented by polynomial-size networks.
  The forward direction is proved by a form of subsampling: from the infinitely many hidden neurons in the mean-field solution, one can select polynomially many representatives and still preserve the learned function on every input simultaneously. At the critical scaling this subsampling has both an ``active'' component, which keeps the data-dependent low-dimensional statistics, and a ``lazy'' component, which resamples the entropy-dominated directions from the prior. Thus the infinite-width mean-field limit gives a clean analytic description of learning without introducing spurious width-dependent generalization power.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的提升算法在通用情况下最优需要O(log(1/ε)/γ²)次弱学习器调用，但作者发现对于满足特定闭包性质的概念类，这个下界可以被绕过，从而追求更高效的算法。

Method: 将目标函数视为消息，对其编码后运行弱学习器得到弱假设（视为损坏的码字），再通过列表解码器获得少量候选强假设，最后用额外样本从中选出正确的强假设。

Result: 对于满足O(log(1/γ))-XOR闭包的概念类F，新算法仅需O(log(1/ε))次弱学习器调用和Õ(log(1/ε)/γ²)个额外样本即可实现强学习。

Conclusion: 首次证明在特定条件下可以突破提升算法的轮数下界，建立了提升算法与列表可解码码之间的新联系。

Abstract: Boosting is a fundamental technique for generically improving the accuracy of learning algorithms (Schapire 1989). Existing boosting algorithms construct a strong learner using $O(\log(\frac{1}ε)/γ^2)$ calls to a $γ$-advantage weak learner, and this round complexity is known to be optimal for generic boosters that succeed on all concept classes (Freund 1995). We show that this lower bound can be circumvented for concept classes that satisfy a mild closure property.
  Specifically, we present a new boosting algorithm that, for any class $\mathcal{F}$ closed under $O(\log \frac{1}γ)$-XOR, strong learns $\mathcal{F}$ using $O(\log \frac{1}ε)$ calls to a $γ$-advantage weak learner and a single batch of $\tilde{O}(\log(\frac{1}ε)/γ^2)$ additional samples.
  Our algorithm arises from a new and simple connection between boosting and list-decodable codes. Viewing the target function as a message, we run the weak learner on its encoding and view the resulting weak hypothesis as a corrupted codeword. Feeding this corrupted codeword to a list decoder, we obtain a small list of candidate hypotheses, at least one of which is a strong hypothesis for the original function. Using additional samples, we identify and output this strong hypothesis.

### [120] [On the convergence of graph Laplacians with a symmetric divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05892)
*Liane Xu*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文证明当流形上配备满足非退化条件的平滑对称散度$D$时，散度$D$与由$D$诱导的黎曼度量$g$对应的测地距离$d_g$平方之间的差值有$O(d_g^4)$阶上界，并论证了这一性质足以保证基于$D$构造的图拉普拉斯算子的逐点收敛性。以Sinkhorn散度在参数化概率测度流形上的应用为例进行说明。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先在光滑紧致连通黎曼子流形上，将测地距离的经典估计推广到任意满足非退化条件的平滑对称散度$D$，证明$|D(p,q)-d_g(p,q)^2| \leq K d_g(p,q)^4$。随后论证该估计足以保证图拉普拉斯算子的逐点收敛性。

Result: 证明了对于任何满足非退化条件的平滑对称散度$D$（其诱导的度量$g_p = \frac{1}{2}\mathrm{Hess}_p(D(p,\cdot))$），散度$D$与测地距离$d_g$的平方之间具有$O(d_g^4)$阶的逼近误差。该性质保证了基于$D$的图拉普拉斯算子逐点收敛。

Conclusion: 该结果将流形学习中关于测地距离的关键估计推广到更一般的散度框架，为使用Sinkhorn散度等非欧氏距离进行流形学习提供了理论支撑，特别是在概率测度流形上的应用。

Abstract: When analyzing a manifold learning algorithm for data lying on a smooth, compact, connected Riemannian submanifold $(\mathcal{M}, g)$ of $\mathbb{R}^d$, a key estimate for the geodesic distance $d_g$ is that there exists $K > 0$ such that $0 \leq d_g(p, q)^2 - \|p-q\|^2 \leq K d_g(p, q)^4$ for all $p, q \in \mathcal{M}$. We observe that more generally, when $\mathcal{M}$ is equipped with a smooth symmetric divergence $D$ satisfying a non-degeneracy condition and $g$ is given by $g_p := \frac{1}{2}\mathrm{Hess}_p(D(p, \cdot))$ for all $p \in \mathcal{M}$, there exists $K > 0$ such that $\left| D(p, q) - d_g(p, q)^2 \right| \leq K d_g(p, q)^4$ for all $p, q \in \mathcal{M}$. As data from scientific experiments become increasingly available, machine learning methods offer a flexible alternative to explicit parametric modelling. We study neural likelihood approximation, where the goal is to learn the likelihood function directly from data without explicit knowledge of the underlying data-generating process. This work improves the theoretical foundations of neural likelihood approximation by alleviating limitations of restrictive model classes: we show that, by working with un-normalized potentials and folding normalization into the training objective, the resulting learning problem is strictly convex.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有经验观察表明，训练后的神经网络在具有组合结构的任务上优于其NTK极限，但缺乏$\textbf{何时}$以及$\textbf{多大}$差距的定量分析。

Method: 引入两个复杂度度量：目标函数的$\textbf{傅里叶复杂度}$（控制NTK回归）和$\textbf{架构复杂度}$（控制深度$L$、宽度$w$、权重变分范数有界$R$的ReLU网络学习）。先刻画架构类$\mathcal{C}_{L,w,R}$的极小极大率（在$L$因子内精确到$Ω(Lw^2R^2/n)$与$\tilde{O}(L^2w^2R^2/n)$之间），再比较NTK估计量与该下界的差距。

Result: 当两种复杂度解耦时（如深度$L$迭代锯齿函数），NTK回归需要$Ω(4^L)$个样本，而极小极大下界是$L$的多项式级。数值实验证实：带限平滑目标上NTK有竞争力，但在超立方体稀疏奇偶模型上，两层网络比NTK测试误差低4-6个数量级。

Conclusion: 差距是函数空间性质——核的平滑偏差与目标的组合结构不匹配，而非核与网络的泛化现象。

Abstract: A persistent empirical observation is that trained neural networks outperform their neural tangent kernel (NTK) limit on tasks with compositional structure, yet a quantitative account of $\textbf{when}$ and $\textbf{by how much}$ has been lacking. Working on the unit circle, we give such an account through a dichotomy between two complexity measures of the target: its $\textbf{Fourier complexity}$, which controls NTK kernel regression, and its $\textbf{architectural complexity}$, which controls learning over depth-$L$, width-$w$ ReLU networks with the variation norm of the weights bounded by $R$. We first characterize the minimax rate of the architecture class $\mathcal{C}_{L,w,R}$, pinning it down up to a single factor of $L$: between $Ω(Lw^2R^2/n)$ and $\tilde{O}(L^2w^2R^2/n)$. We then show the NTK estimator sits $\textbf{exponentially}$ above this floor whenever the two complexities decouple: for the depth-$L$ iterated sawtooth, NTK regression needs $Ω(4^L)$ samples while the minimax floor is polynomial in $L$. Numerical experiments confirm the theoretical claims: on bandlimited smooth targets, the NTK is competitive or better, while on the hypercube sparse-parity model, a standard two-layer network beats the NTK by four to six orders of magnitude in test error. The gap is thus a function-space property, a mismatch between the kernel's smoothness bias and the target's compositional structure, rather than a generic kernel-versus-network phenomenon.

</details>

### [124] [Retrieval over Reasoning: A Cost-Controlled Benchmark of Language Models for Energy-Retrofit Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05440)
*Eliseo Curcio*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文研究了建筑节能措施(ECM)推荐问题，在10,422份纽约市真实能源审计记录上，比较了传统机器学习模型和大语言模型(LLM)的性能。主要发现：梯度提升树在ECM推荐上表现优于神经网络；将任务框架从单标签分类改为多标签分类显著提升性能；检索增强生成(RAG)可稳定提升LLM性能(+0.11到+0.20 micro-F1)，而显式推理仅增加成本无精度提升；70B参数开源模型配合简单检索步骤可达与前沿模型相当的性能，成本仅为后者的1/10。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建筑节能措施(ECM)推荐是一个结构化的多标签预测问题，现有监督模型训练信号弱，通用语言模型缺乏对本地建筑存量的理解。作者希望利用真实世界的大规模能源审计数据来解决这一实际需求。

Method: 使用10,422份纽约市LL87能源审计记录，对比了15种监督学习模型（包括树集成和神经网络）以及8种LLM（来自4个提供商），采用2x2实验设计独立控制检索增强(RAG)和显式推理，评估指标包括micro-F1、成本和延迟。

Result: 树集成在EUI预测上优于所有神经网络（R²=0.757）；将任务重框架为多标签分类使micro-F1从0.259提升至0.571；RAG稳定提升LLM性能(+0.11~+0.20 micro-F1)，显式推理无精度提升（-0.018~+0.010）但成本高达8.4倍；70B开源模型+检索达0.511 micro-F1，成本为前沿模型的1/10。

Conclusion: 对于ECM推荐任务，传统梯度提升树结合恰当的任务框架仍是最优选择；LLM倾向于过度推荐（高召回低精度），检索增强可有效改善精度；在成本和性能之间，开源小模型配合检索增强可达到实用水平，性价比远优于闭源大模型。

Abstract: Recommending the correct set of energy conservation measures (ECMs) for a building is a structured, multi-label prediction problem in which a task-specific supervised model has weak training signal and a general language model has no grounding in the local building stock. We study this problem on 10,422 real New York City Local Law 87 (LL87) energy-audit records, taking as ground truth the set of ECM categories that certified auditors actually recommended. We make four contributions. First, we establish that energy-use-intensity (EUI) prediction - the upstream task - is effectively solved by tree ensembles: across fifteen trained models, a stacking ensemble reaches a coefficient of determination R^2 = 0.757, and every one of six neural architectures is outperformed by gradient-boosted trees. Second, we show that the framing of the recommendation task dominates model choice: recasting ECM recommendation as 19-way multi-label classification rather than single-label categorization lifts a gradient-boosted-tree baseline from a previously reported 25.9% accuracy to a micro-F1 of 0.571. Third, we benchmark eight large language models (LLMs) from four providers in a 2x2 design that independently toggles retrieval grounding and explicit reasoning, scoring each arm on per-label F1, U.S.-dollar cost per building, and latency; retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) improves micro-F1 by +0.11 to +0.20 on every model, while explicit reasoning yields no measurable accuracy change (-0.018 to +0.010) at up to 8.4x the cost. Fourth, we show LLMs systematically over-recommend - high recall, low precision - and that retrieval closes the gap chiefly by improving precision. A 70-billion-parameter open-weight model with a fifteen-line nearest-neighbor retrieval step reaches 0.511 micro-F1 at $0.00032 per building, comparable to a frontier model at roughly 10.1x lower cost.

</details>


### [125] [Empirical Global Games of Regime Change](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05534)
*Matthew J. Baker,Khaled Eltokhy,Weichao Guo*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个可估计的全球博弈模型来分析政变，将战略协调纳入实证研究，区分了政变的可行性（政权强度）与合意性（叛乱的感知收益），并可通过模拟极大似然估计参数，进行反事实分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有政变实证研究多采用简化形式方法，隐含地处理协调问题，缺乏对多重均衡下战略互动的明确建模。本文旨在桥接全球博弈理论与政变实证文献，提供一个可估计的协调博弈模型。

Method: 基于全球博弈框架构建政变的结构化模型，将政权强度与叛乱收益作为可观测基本面的函数，并利用均衡选择机制区分可行性与合意性。采用模拟极大似然估计结合压缩映射进行参数估计。

Result: 模型能够将政变结果分解为可行性（政权强度）和合意性（叛乱收益）两个组成部分，在可获得政变力量信息时还可估计行动者对政权强度的不确定性。通过反事实分析，可以考察政变收益、政权强度和信息质量变化的影响。

Conclusion: 该框架为政变的实证分析提供了理论基础，能够通过排除性约束和均衡假设分离不同机制的作用，并为政策反事实分析提供了工具。

Abstract: Global games theory provides a tractable framework for analyzing coordination problems with multiple equilibria, with regime overthrow serving as a canonical application. A large empirical literature on coups d'état examines the relationship between country-level characteristics, coup occurrence, and coup success using reduced-form approaches that leave the underlying coordination problem implicit. Bridging these literatures, we develop an estimable global games model of coups d'état. The model incorporates strategic coordination into the empirical analysis of coups, employing the global games framework as an equilibrium selection device. The model distinguishes between the feasibility and desirability of regime overthrow, allowing observable fundamentals to enter separately into beliefs about regime strength and perceived gains from rebellion. The model therefore provides a theoretical basis for decomposing coup outcomes into feasibility and desirability components under maintained exclusion restrictions and equilibrium assumptions. If information on coup strength is available, the model also allows estimation of agents' uncertainty about regime strength. We show how the model can be estimated using simulated maximum likelihood coupled with a contraction mapping, and demonstrate how observable covariates map into regime strength and the perceived benefits of overthrow. We illustrate how the framework can be applied through counterfactuals varying coup benefits, regime strength, and information quality.

</details>

Abstract: This paper proposes to project and expand the conditional mean function of the structural error given the regressors in an endogenous regression under consideration. As the projection process is semiparametric, we define this procedure as a semiparametric projection (SP) method to address endogeneity in regression models by internally constructed instrumental variables. The SP method is applicable to many classes of regression models associated with endogeneity, such as linear, nonlinear, and non- and semi-parametric models, and provides a simple and computationally tractable alternative to conventional instrumental variable approaches available from the existing literature. It then proposes a simple LASSO selection method to examine the finite-sample performance of both the proposed method and the established theory by simulated and real data examples.

### [127] [A Framework for Transportation and Land Use Integration as a Parallel Constrained Multiple Discrete-Continuous Extreme Value (PC-MDCEV) Home Production Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05862)
*Jason Hawkins,Khandker Nurul Habib*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文基于家庭生产理论，提出了一个微观经济学基础的交通与土地利用选择模型集成方法。通过引入并行约束的多重离散-连续极值（MDCEV）结构来建模多成员家庭，并将旅行时间定义为开展活动所需的最小时间，从时间预算中扣除。基于大多伦多地区的合成数据实证验证，发现家庭生产中存在时间规模经济，且住宅类型显著影响时间使用和消费模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统综合城市模型（IUM）仅通过可达性或旅行时间来连接交通与土地利用系统，未能充分捕捉家庭在有限时间和货币预算之间的权衡。作者希望建立一个更完整的微观经济基础，以更好地反映家庭决策的复杂性。

Method: 基于家庭生产理论构建效用函数，兼顾家庭货币支出和个人时间使用。创新点包括：(1) 引入并行约束的MDCEV结构，支持多成员家庭建模；(2) 将旅行时间定义为开展活动所需的最小时间，从时间预算中扣除，并将其作为可达性度量。使用大多伦多地区合成数据集进行实证验证。

Result: 实证结果表明：(1) 家庭生产中存在时间使用的规模经济效应，类似于市场生产中的规模效应；(2) 住宅类型（独立屋、公寓等）对时间使用和消费模式有显著影响。

Conclusion: 提出的基于家庭生产理论的集成模型能更全面地捕捉家庭在时间和金钱预算之间的权衡，为未来城市建模实践提供了改进方向，以更好地理解家庭决策的复杂动态。

Abstract: Integrated urban models (IUM) typically rely on a measure of accessibility or travel time to form the link between the transportation and land use systems. Such integration does not fully capture the trade-offs made by households in how they spend their limited temporal and monetary budgets. We propose a microeconomic foundation for transportation and land use choice model integration based on the theory of home production. A utility function is developed that considers both household monetary expenditure and individual time use. We address several limitations in previous home production functions. First, the introduction of a parallel constrained multiple discrete-continuous extreme value (MDCEV) structure that allows for the inclusion of multi-person households in the model. Second, travel time is defined as the minimum time required to conduct an activity and deducted from the temporal budget. This assumption has several appealing features. It defines the minimum time to complete an activity as a measure of accessibility. An empirical application is provided for the Greater Toronto Area using a validated synthetic dataset. Empirical results demonstrate an economy of scale in time devoted to home production, analogous to scaling exhibit in market production. It was found that the mix of dwelling types (detached, apartment, etc.) has a significant influence on both time use and consumption. Finally, we provide several directions for future research to advance the practice of urban modelling and better capture the complex dynamics of household decision-making.

### [128] [Bolivia and an IMF Extended Fund Facility: Financial Sustainability, Verifiable Social Sustainability, and Net Financing Additionality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05878)
*Ricardo Alonzo Fernández Salguero*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文评估玻利维亚在外部融资压力下的稳定方案，通过联合建模财政可持续性、可验证的社会可持续性以及多边融资的净增量效应。核心修正在于：已获得、已签约或预期将从多边机构获得的融资不能算作IMF扩展基金安排的边际收益，只有增量、流动、及时且未被替代的融资才被计入。结果不支持正统的IMF优先战略或前置财政紧缩，最优方案是附带净增量、生产性执行、社会健康底线和保护贫困与母婴指标的优惠多边融资组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献在评估外部融资压力下的稳定方案时，常忽略已确保融资的边际增量效应，也未将财政可持续性与社会可持续性（贫困、不平等、母婴健康）联合建模，导致对IMF优先战略和财政紧缩方案的评价可能失真。

Method: 采用联合建模框架，将已确保融资移入基准线，仅奖励增量、流动、及时且非替代性的融资；结合修正后的方案评分、贫困与不平等指标、母婴死亡率指标、公共投资乘数、自我挫败式紧缩诊断、蒙特卡洛不确定性分析、留一准则检验及不利执行假设。

Result: 不支持正统的IMF优先战略或前置财政紧缩；最优方案是具备净增量、生产性执行、社会健康底线及防止贫困与母婴恶化的优惠多边融资组合；IMF安排只有在能增加未确保资源或可信度时才有价值。

Conclusion: 可持续性必须作为财政与社会条件的联合状态来评估：通过削弱增长、贫困、不平等或母婴健康来填补资金缺口，在宏观经济上是自我挫败的。

Abstract: This paper evaluates stabilization scenarios for Bolivia under external-financing stress by jointly modeling financial sustainability, verifiable social sustainability and the net additionality of multilateral financing. The main correction is that financing already received, contracted or expected from multilateral institutions cannot be counted as a marginal benefit of a hypothetical IMF Extended Fund Facility. Already secured resources are moved to the baseline; only incremental, liquid, timely and non-displaced financing is rewarded. The analysis combines corrected scenario scoring, poverty and inequality measures, maternal-child mortality indicators, public investment multipliers, self-defeating consolidation diagnostics, Monte Carlo uncertainty, leave-one-criterion-out tests and adverse execution assumptions. The results do not support an orthodox IMF-first strategy or front-loaded fiscal consolidation. The strongest designs are concessional multilateral packages with verified net additionality, productive execution, social-health floors and protection against poverty and maternal-child deterioration. An IMF arrangement is valuable only if it adds resources or credibility that were not already secured. The conclusion is that sustainability must be evaluated as a joint financial and social condition: closing cash gaps by weakening growth, poverty, inequality or maternal-child outcomes can be macroeconomically self-defeating.

</details>


### [129] [Revision Risk in Real-Time Macroeconomic Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05882)
*Yizhou,Kuang*

Main category: econ.EM

TL;DR: 本文研究宏观经济预测中数据修订的风险，发现初次发布到约180天的修订占实际活动目标后期误差MSE的8.3%，通胀目标占3.6%，并提出在实时环境下利用部分识别信息进行不确定性量化的多种传输方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宏观经济预测的最终结果是先发布后修订的，不同时间点的预测区间代表不同的不确定性。现有方法常忽略修订风险，且后期结果的误差样本稀缺，难以直接校准。作者希望理清修订风险在整个发布周期中的演化规律，并探索如何在实时环境下有效量化这种不确定性。

Method: 将后期结果的MSE分解为初步预测风险、修订风险及其协方差。利用SPF数据实证分析修订贡献。基于部分识别框架，利用已发布历史获取早期误差和修订的边缘分布，但允许其依赖结构未知，从而得到Frechet-Makarov边界集。提出直接后期校准、依赖稳健传输、符号或修订模型传输等方法。

Result: 首次发布至约180天的修订对实际活动目标后期MSE的贡献为8.3%，对通胀目标为3.6%。部分识别框架产生尖锐的Frechet-Makarov集。样本外结果表明没有通用的传输规则，方法选择取决于覆盖率和稳定性。

Conclusion: 修订风险是宏观经济预测不确定性的重要组成部分，且不同目标类型差异显著。后期不确定性可被部分识别，多种传输方法各有适用场景，需根据覆盖率和稳定性进行选择，而非采用统一规则。

Abstract: Macroeconomic forecasts refer to outcomes that are first released and then revised. A 90 percent interval for the first GDP release, a six-month value, or a latest-value benchmark is not the same uncertainty statement. We ask how revision risk evolves through the release cycle and what can be reported in real time when later-outcome errors are scarce. We decompose later-outcome MSE into preliminary forecast risk, revision risk, and their covariance. In SPF data, first-release to roughly 180-day revisions account for 8.3 percent of later-outcome MSE across real-activity targets, versus 3.6 percent across inflation targets. We show that later-outcome uncertainty is partially identified: released histories give early-error and revision marginals, but not their dependence. This yields a sharp Frechet-Makarov set and motivates direct late calibration, dependence-robust transport, and signed or revision-model transport. Out-of-sample results support method choice rather than a universal transport rule: coverage and stability determine when transport gains are usable.

### [131] [A Machine-Learning-Compatible Omnibus Test for Treatment Effect Heterogeneity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06412)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有处理效应异质性检验方法通常依赖于特定模型假设或计算成本高，缺乏一个兼容现代机器学习估计器、形式化且计算高效的通用非参数检验框架。

Method: 提出一种非参数整体检验统计量，推导其渐近零分布，并开发一种避免每次迭代重估 nuisance 参数的高效自助法；方法适用于随机实验、选择变量可观测、双重差分和工具变量等多种识别策略。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟显示检验在零假设下接近名义大小，对异质性备择假设具有良好的检验功效；两个实证应用（退休储蓄和贸易自由化）进一步验证了方法的实用性。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个灵活、计算高效且理论完善的异质性检验工具，填补了现代因果推断中非参数整体检验的空白，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: This study proposes a formal, computationally efficient nonparametric omnibus test for treatment-effect heterogeneity that is compatible with a broad class of estimators, including modern machine-learning methods. The test is designed for settings in which identification can rely on high-dimensional controls while heterogeneity is assessed with respect to a low-dimensional subset of covariates. We derive the test statistic's asymptotic null distribution and develop a bootstrap procedure that is efficient because it avoids re-estimating nuisance parameters in each iteration. The testing approach applies to multiple empirical designs, including randomized experiments, selection-on-observables, difference-in-differences, and instrumental-variables settings. Monte Carlo simulations show that the test attains near-nominal size under the null and exhibits good power against heterogeneous alternatives. We further illustrate the procedure using two empirical applications on retirement savings and trade liberalization.

</details>

### [132] [Arbitrage-Free Multi-Maturity Risk-Neutral Marginals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06204)
*Hao Qin,Ruozhong Yang,Charlie Che,Liming Feng*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从无套利期权价格显式构造风险中性边际分布的通用方法，该方法在观测区间内逐区间分配概率质量以精确复现期权价格，在区间外使用幂律尾部完成分布，确保无蝶式套利和日历套利，并支持密度、分布函数、分位数和蒙特卡洛采样的高效计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常只针对特定目的优化部分属性，缺乏一种能同时满足所有需求（精确复现期权价格、无套利、全支撑概率律、高效评估与采样）的通用构造方法，导致上游无套利期权价格与下游应用所需的可用风险中性边际之间存在缺口。

Method: 在观测行权价范围内，逐区间分配概率质量以精确匹配输入期权价格；在观测范围外，通过闭式幂律尾部满足价格和斜率边界条件，分配剩余概率质量。通过构造保证无蝶式套利和日历套利。

Result: 在合成SSVI数据和S&P 500市场数据上的数值实验表明，所提出的构造方法能够高效且稳健地生成满足所有上述属性的边际分布。

Conclusion: 该构造方法在设计中保证可行性，计算高效，且得到的边际分布具有闭式密度、分布函数、分位数，并支持高效蒙特卡洛采样，填补了上游期权价格与下游应用之间的缺口。

Abstract: Many quantitative finance methods and applications are formulated in terms of option-implied risk-neutral marginals rather than directly in terms of option prices. Representative examples include martingale optimal transport, Bass local-volatility calibration, scenario analysis, and option-implied tail-risk measurement. The desired risk-neutral marginals should define a genuine probability law on the entire support, reproduce the input arbitrage-free option prices exactly, be free of butterfly and calendar arbitrage, and admit efficient evaluation of the density, distribution function, and quantiles, as well as Monte Carlo sampling. Existing methods typically optimize only a subset of these properties, depending on their intended purpose. This leaves a gap between upstream arbitrage-free option prices and the readily usable risk-neutral marginals required by downstream applications. We propose an explicit construction of risk-neutral marginals from discrete arbitrage-free option prices. On the observed strike range, probability mass is assigned interval by interval to exactly reproduce the input option prices. Outside the observed range, closed-form power-law tails complete the distribution by satisfying price and slope boundary conditions and allocating the remaining probability mass. Butterfly- and calendar-arbitrage-freeness are guaranteed by construction. The construction is feasible by design and computationally efficient. The resulting marginal laws admit closed-form densities, distribution functions, quantiles, and efficient Monte Carlo sampling. Numerical experiments on synthetic SSVI data and S\&P~500 market data demonstrate that the proposed construction efficiently and robustly produces marginals satisfying all of these properties in practice.

</details>


### [133] [Signature-based identification of volatility models from path geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06340)
*Òscar Burés,Rafael De Santiago*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于路径签名的框架，通过梯度提升分类器从观测路径数据中识别随机波动率模型类别，无需参数校准，并在多种设定下实现了高分类精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机波动率模型识别依赖参数校准，缺乏直接从路径数据中识别模型类别的有效方法。

Method: 利用截断路径签名将波动率轨迹映射到特征空间，结合梯度提升分类器进行模型分类。

Result: 在多种模型设定下实现高分类准确率；可区分Hurst参数相近的粗糙波动率模型；在参数不确定性下仍有效；前四级签名捕获了大部分判别信息，高阶项改进有限。

Conclusion: 随机波动率模型可以通过样本路径的几何特征有效识别。

Abstract: We propose a signature-based framework for the identification of stochastic volatility model classes from observed path data. By mapping volatility trajectories into a feature space via truncated path signatures and applying a gradient boosting classifier, we show that it is possible to distinguish between different classes of volatility dynamics without relying on parametric calibration.
  Through a series of numerical experiments, we demonstrate that the method achieves high classification accuracy across a range of settings, from structurally distinct models to cases involving rough volatility models with closely spaced Hurst parameters. We show that the method remains effective under parameter uncertainty, where each simulated path is drawn with randomly sampled model parameters, and provide a detailed analysis of the misclassification pattern between the Heston and Ornstein--Uhlenbeck models in terms of the volatility of volatility parameter. The results highlight that most of the relevant discriminative information is captured by the first four levels of the signature, while higher-order terms provide only marginal improvements. Overall, the findings support the view that stochastic volatility models can be effectively identified through the geometry of their sample paths.

### [134] [What Useful Alphas?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06502)
*Andrew Y. Chen,Ivo Welch*

Main category: q-fin.GN

TL;DR: 本文检验了约200个已发表的长期-短期异常股票组合，发现其收益在2005年后大幅下降，尤其对非微型股而言，经考虑交易成本和运气因素后收益几乎为零。结论是：在21世纪，这些异常对非小微市值组合管理已无实际价值，公开股票市场非常有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证学术界发现的市场异常（如规模、价值、动量等因子）是否在近年仍能为实际投资者带来超额收益，尤其是排除微型股后的实盘可行性。

Method: 基于Chen and Zimmermann (2022)的约200个已发表异常组合数据，分别检验不同时间段（截至2005年 vs. 2006年后）和不同市值范围（全市场 vs. 剔除微型股后的前3000只股票）下的零投资组合月度收益。

Result: 截至2005年，中位数零投资组合月收益为48bp；2006年后下降至19bp；仅考虑非微型股（市值前90%）为26bp；同时限定2006年后且非微型股则骤降至7bp；考虑交易成本和运气后，这7bp也被消除。

Conclusion: 已发表的学术异常策略在21世纪对非微型股组合管理已无实际价值，市场总体上非常有效。

Abstract: This paper examines about 200 published long-short anomaly equity portfolios (Chen and Zimmermann, 2022). Over the period through 2005 (December 2005 and earlier) and across all stocks, their median zero-investment return was an impressive 48 bp per month. Using only post-2005 years (January 2006 onward) reduces this to 19 bp. Using only "non-micro" top-3,000 stocks in the top 90% of market capitalization reduces this to 26 bp. Using only post-2005 and non-micro stocks reduces this to 7 bp. Even modest allowances for luck or transaction costs would have eliminated even these 7 bp. The evidence strongly suggests that published academic anomalies have been useless to non-micro-cap portfolio managers in the 21st century. Public stock markets were very efficient.

</details>

### [136] [AI tools in Arab University English classrooms: Looking back and forward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05403)
*Mohammed Q. Shormani,Muneef Yehia Alshawsh*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用PRISMA系统综述方法，在Google Scholar、Web of Science和Scopus三大数据库中检索2023年1月至2025年8月期间的文献。初始检索到184篇，经筛选最终纳入11篇符合标准的已发表实证研究。

Result: EL2学习者对AI工具持积极态度，AI在起草、修订和练习等环节有助益。但实证提升主要集中在表面层级的写作结果上；高阶写作质量和口语熟练度的改进效果参差不齐，且往往需要教师中介才能奏效。

Conclusion: 提出针对阿拉伯大学AI融入EL2教学的研究议程和实操指南，强调需要阶梯式整合、教师培训以及反思性任务设计，以减少学习者对AI工具的过度依赖。

Abstract: This paper aims to synthesize empirical research on AI tools used to support English as a second/foreign language (EL2) learners in Arab University classrooms (AUCs) between Jan 1st 2023 and Aug 31st 2025. We utilized 3 large datasets, namely Google Scholar, Web of Science, and Scopus as the data sources. Using PRISMA-guided searches across these well-known databases, we included only published articles. The search process results in 184 studies, but only 11 studies met the inclusion criteria. Findings unveil that EL2 learners have positive attitudes towards AI for drafting, revision, and practice. Empirical gains were most consistent for surface-level outcomes improvements in higher-order writing quality and speaking proficiency was mixed and often contingent on teacher mediation. The paper concludes by proposing a research agenda and practical guidelines for Arab universities seeking evidence-based AI integration in EL2 instruction. It also recommends scaffolded integration, teacher training, reflective tasks to reduce over-reliance on AI tools.

### [137] [The Jagged Global Economy: Frontier AI Unevenly Exposes National Economies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05404)
*Arul Murugan,Tomás Aguirre,Abhishek Nagaraj,Rishi Bommasani*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文构建了涵盖141个国家的AI暴露度指标，发现高收入国家比低收入国家暴露度更高，女性比男性暴露度更高，并通过跨国汇款机制揭示了间接暴露效应，表明各国AI暴露差异巨大，不能简单套用美欧政策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多聚焦于少数高收入经济体，缺乏对全球各国（尤其是低收入国家）AI暴露程度的系统性评估，无法支持差异化的政策制定。

Method: 结合职业层面的AI暴露分数与141个国家的就业数据构建国家AI暴露度指标；利用Anthropic、Microsoft、OpenAI的AI采用统计数据验证指标有效性；引入跨境汇款依赖机制计算间接暴露度。

Result: 高收入国家暴露度显著高于低收入国家；欧洲和中亚比撒哈拉以南非洲暴露度高50%；91%的国家中女性暴露度高于男性；塔吉克斯坦因依赖俄罗斯汇款，间接暴露度从低于平均水平变为高于平均水平。

Conclusion: 各国AI暴露度差异巨大，基于美国或欧洲劳动力市场制定的政策无法直接推广到其他国家。

Abstract: Frontier AI's labor-market effects matter to workers, firms, and policymakers, but current evidence generally comes from a handful of high-income economies. The capabilities of frontier AI are jagged across work tasks and national economies diverge in how they allocate human labor. We introduce a national AI exposure metric that combines occupation-level exposure scores and international employment data for 141 countries. We find that high income countries are substantially more exposed than low income countries and that Europe and Central Asia are 50 percent more exposed than Sub-Saharan Africa. We also find a gender gap: women are more exposed than men in 91 percent of countries, driven by their concentration in white-collar and sales occupations. The exceptions are countries where women's employment remains concentrated in agriculture and household enterprises. We validate our national AI exposure estimates by showing they predict national AI adoption statistics published by Anthropic, Microsoft, and OpenAI. Beyond direct exposure, we identify a new mechanism for indirect exposure due to cross-country income dependencies. Some nations such as Tajikistan depend heavily on foreign workers remitting money back to their home countries: Tajikistan's direct exposure to frontier AI is below-average but because 37 percent of Tajikistan GDP is Russian remittance and Russia is very exposed, Tajikistan's remittance-accounted exposure becomes above-average. Our research shows that national variation in exposure is large enough that policy responses calibrated to U.S. or European labor markets will not generalize.

</details>


### [138] [CCBENCH: Assessing LLM Cultural Competence via Implicitly Signaled Norms using Health Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05405)
*Vasudha Varadarajan,Akhila Yerukola,Mona T. Diab,Maarten Sap*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出CCBENCH框架，用于评估大语言模型的文化能力（将文化视为规范遵守状态的连续体而非二元分类）。以医疗健康为案例创建CCBENCH-Health数据集，包含6种文化、60个角色、3,120次交互。测试五个领先模型，最佳模型仅20-30%能给出文化适切回应；显式提示文化线索（CoT）仅提升3-5%；模型更倾向顺应自身内置偏见而非适应文化线索，尤其在阿富汗语境中表现最差（8.8%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI模型缺乏文化能力，容易基于刻板印象而非用户隐含的文化价值观进行交互；且已有研究多将文化视为静态二元归属，忽视文化规范的连续性和情境性。

Method: 构建CCBENCH框架，将文化定义为规范遵守状态的连续体；创建CCBENCH-Health数据集，涵盖6种文化、60个角色（每种文化10个角色，展现不同规范遵守程度），每个角色在18个真实对话场景中回答52个医疗问题，共3,120次交互；评估五个主流LLM并引入CoT提示策略。

Result: 最佳模型仅20-30%产生文化适切回应；CoT提示提升约3-5%；模型对"规避文化规范"的角色表现更好，呈现不对称性；阿富汗语境表现最差（8.8%）；模型对隐含文化风格的适应优于显性文化实践。

Conclusion: 当前LLM文化能力严重不足，模型存在内置偏见优先于文化适应的系统性偏差，文化适应效果因文化背景和规范表达方式（显性vs隐性）而异，亟需改进模型的文化感知与适应能力。

Abstract: To interact with users fairly and without stereotyping, AI models must display cultural competency, i.e., the ability to infer and adapt to a user's implicitly signaled cultural values, rather than relying on static demographic traits. We introduce CCBENCH, a framework for evaluating cultural competency in large language models (LLMs), treating culture as a continuum of norm adherence states rather than as a binary state of cultural belongingness. As a case study on health, we create CCBENCH-Health, which includes 60 theoretically grounded personas exhibiting varied norm-adherence states across six cultures, each engaging in 18 realistic dialogues. Each persona is evaluated on 52 authentic healthcare questions drawn from real user forums, yielding 3,120 unique interactions. Benchmarking five leading models reveals that even the best achieve culturally appropriate responses only 20-30% of the time. When explicitly prompted to focus on culturally relevant cues from the conversational history (CoT), performance improves modestly by 3-5% on average. We find that models perform best when personas avoid cultural norms rather than follow them, revealing a persistent asymmetry, suggesting a preference in the models to align with built-in biases than adapt to cultural cues. This is especially observed in the Afghan context (Avg: 8.8%), where cultural cues rarely yield appropriate health advice. Finally, we find that models sometimes adapt more readily to implicit, cultural conversational styles than to explicitly stated cultural practices, though this varies across cultures.

</details>

The initial framework, built on Design Thinking and INTERACT, was validated through a CORDTRA interaction analysis of three teachers and four faculty mentors in an eight-week workshop to derive the final framework. ### [140] [Position: Preventing AI-Generated CSAM Necessitates New Approaches to AI Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05407)
*Neil Kale,Rebecca Portnoff,Pratiksha Thaker,Michael Simpson,Robertson Wang,Kevin Kuo,Chhavi Yadav,Virginia Smith*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文指出现有AI安全技术因伦理和法律约束（如无法接触儿童性虐待材料）而难以应对AI助长的儿童性侵问题，提出了15个开放问题，并呼吁将儿童保护作为AI安全的核心维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代AI系统被滥用于生成儿童性虐待材料、实施儿童性剥削，而现有AI安全技术因数据可访问性、透明度和评估实践与儿童性虐待材料相关的伦理法律约束不兼容，无法有效应对这一威胁。

Method: 通过分析伦理法律约束带来的技术挑战（如数据集审计、红队测试、微调预防的限制），系统梳理了AI开发生命周期中的15个开放问题，并提出面向研究者、开发者和政策制定者的针对性建议。

Result: 识别出15个在线儿童性剥削与虐待的开放问题，覆盖数据集构建、模型设计、部署到长期维护全流程。

Conclusion: 防止AI助长儿童性虐待应被视为AI安全的核心维度，需要将负责任的AI原则转化为具体防护措施，缩小理论AI安全与儿童保护现实之间的差距。

Abstract: Modern artificial intelligence (AI) systems present profound new risks to child safety. AI is increasingly being misused to create AI-generated child sexual abuse material, facilitate child sexual exploitation, and reduce barriers to harm. In this paper, we argue that protecting children from AI-facilitated sexual abuse requires new approaches to AI safety. Existing safety techniques assume data accessibility, transparency, and evaluation practices that are incompatible with the ethical and legal constraints surrounding child sexual abuse material. We examine how these constraints create new technical challenges, such as limitations on dataset auditing, red teaming, and fine-tuning prevention. In turn, we outline *15 open problems* in online child sexual exploitation and abuse across the AI development lifecycle, from dataset curation and model design to deployment and long-term maintenance. We propose targeted recommendations for researchers, developers, and policymakers to bridge the gap between theoretical AI safety and the realities of child protection. Our work aims to reframe preventing AI-facilitated child sexual abuse as a central, safety-critical dimension for AI research, motivating work that translates responsible AI principles into concrete safeguards against the exploitation of children.

### [141] [Life Cycle Assessment of Pre-training the Lucie 7B Open-Source Large Language Model on the Jean Zay Supercomputer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05408)
*Marc Léobet,Pierre-François Lavallée,Jean-Pierre Lorré*

Main category: cs.CY

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The environmental impact of training large language models (LLMs) is increasingly scrutinised, yet most published estimates focus on operational energy and disclose little about manufacturing (embodied) emissions, water consumption, or the underlying highperformance computing (HPC) infrastructure. The assessment is framed by the AFNOR SPEC 2314 "Frugal AI" reference and applies the Labos 1point5 methodology for greenhouse gas(GHG) accounting in computing. The study scope extends from data preparation to model validation, and integrates the full life cycle of the hardware infrastructure: manufacturing (including raw-material extraction), use (compute, temporary storage, system administration, cooling), and end-of-life. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编程学习资源丰富但人工整理耗时费力，缺乏自动化的方式将概念相似的代码活动组织在一起，难以实现规模化、教学上有意义的资源推荐。

Method: 从每个代码样本中提取基于模式的KCs，通过计算各学习活动关联的KC集合间的相似度，识别目标概念相近的教学资源，实现上下文相关且教学合理的推荐。

Result: 在专家整理的Python入门语料库上，基于模式KCs的方法检索到的资源与专家组织一致，且在标准排序评估中优于代表性KCs基线和嵌入基线。

Abstract: Introductory programming instruction relies on hands-on practice and short learning activities to support mastery of foundational concepts. Although many such learning resources exist, organizing and linking these items in instructionally meaningful ways is challenging without time-intensive expert curation. This study investigates the use of pattern-based Knowledge Components (KCs) to automatically identify code-based learning resources targeting similar concepts. In our approach, pattern-based KCs are extracted from each code sample, and related activities are identified by measuring similarity between the KC sets associated with each activity. By leveraging alignment at the level of semantically important programming patterns, this method supports contextually appropriate and pedagogically useful recommendations. We evaluate our approach on an expert-organized corpus of introductory Python materials in which instructors grouped items into bundles based on conceptual similarity. Results show that our pattern-based KC approach retrieves resources that align with this expert organization, and outperformed representative KC- and embedding-based baselines across standard ranking evaluations. Overall, the framework supports targeted, concept-oriented guidance for programming learners and can help instructors organize, bundle, and recommend instructional content at scale.

### [143] [CANONIC: Governance Is Compilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05410)
*Dexter Hadley*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: CANONIC是一个受编译器理论启发的治理框架，通过三个公理（三元组、继承、内省）对应编译器的语法、作用域解析和类型系统层，对数字制品进行结构化准入检查。研究表明，结构化的准入检查无法可靠区分"slop"（不可靠内容），slop不是算法可计算的属性，而是领域专家的判断结果。因此CANONIC的价值不在于过滤内容，而在于构建可审计、可复现的证据账本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型生成内容的速度远超人工核查能力，导致"slop"（劣质/不可靠内容）泛滥。牛津词典将"slop"评为2025年度词汇，反映出这一问题已受到广泛关注。现有方法缺乏系统性的治理机制来管控哪些内容可以进入语料库。

Method: 借鉴编译器理论，将内容治理建模为三个层次：Triad（语法层，对应语法分析）、Inheritance（作用域解析层）、Introspection（类型系统层）。准入判定是可判定的线性时间检查。通过跨四个制度（regimes）的预注册跨提供商基准测试来评估结构准入的有效性。

Result: 结构化的准入检查无法可靠地将可靠内容与不可靠内容（slop）区分开。没有一种基于文本阅读的门控机制能够可靠地分离可靠与不可靠内容。

Conclusion: Slop不是算法可以计算的属性，而是领域专家的判断结果。治理层的价值不在于判定什么是slop，而在于保持记录的可审计性——每个声明都锚定到定义、提交记录和证据窗口，实现端到端的可复现和可核查。

Abstract: We present CANONIC: governed intelligence that compiles digital artifacts into an evidence ledger at scale. Large language models generate prose faster than anyone can check it, the failure Oxford Languages named 'slop', its 2025 Word of the Year. CANONIC governs whether content may enter a corpus the way a compiler decides whether a program is well-formed: mechanically, by a grammar, at the boundary of admission. Governance reduces to three axioms (Triad, Inheritance, Introspection) that map one-to-one onto compiler theory's syntax, scope-resolution, and type-system layers, and admission is a decidable, linear-time check. We then ask, with a pre-registered cross-provider benchmark across four regimes, whether structural admission keeps slop out. It does not: no prose-reading gate reliably separates reliable from unreliable content. Slop is not a property an algorithm computes. It is a verdict of domain expertise. So a governance layer does not decide slop; it keeps the record auditable -- every claim anchored to a definition, a commit, and an evidence window, reproducible and checkable end to end.

</details>


### [144] [The GenAI Skill Bypass: Mapping Divergent Pathways of University Students and Staff AI Literacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05411)
*Eduardo Oliveira,Narelle English,Tracii Ryan,Kamila Misiejuk,Cory dal Ponte,Sonsoles López-Pernas,Mohammed Saqr*
